<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">The Claude Agent SDK provides detailed token usage information for each interaction with Claude. This guide explains how to properly track costs and understand usage reporting, especially when dealing with parallel tool uses and multi-step conversations.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">For complete API documentation, see the <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/agent-sdk/typescript">TypeScript SDK reference</a>.</p>

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">When Claude processes requests, it reports token usage at the message level. This usage data is essential for tracking costs and billing users appropriately.</p>

<ol class="list-none pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item]">
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Steps</strong>: A step is a single request/response pair between your application and Claude</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Messages</strong>: Individual messages within a step (text, tool uses, tool results)</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Usage</strong>: Token consumption data attached to assistant messages</li>
</ol>

<h3 class="text-xl font-medium mb-2 text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6" id="single-vs-parallel-tool-use"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex

          font-base

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">When Claude executes tools, the usage reporting differs based on whether tools are executed sequentially or in parallel:</p>

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Here&#x27;s how messages and usage are reported in a typical multi-step conversation:</p>
<div class="group relative my-5 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><pre class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><code>&lt;!-- Step 1: Initial request with parallel tool uses --&gt;
assistant (text)      { id: &quot;msg_1&quot;, usage: { output_tokens: 100, ... } }
assistant (tool_use)  { id: &quot;msg_1&quot;, usage: { output_tokens: 100, ... } }
assistant (tool_use)  { id: &quot;msg_1&quot;, usage: { output_tokens: 100, ... } }
assistant (tool_use)  { id: &quot;msg_1&quot;, usage: { output_tokens: 100, ... } }
user (tool_result)
user (tool_result)
user (tool_result)

&lt;!-- Step 2: Follow-up response --&gt;
assistant (text)      { id: &quot;msg_2&quot;, usage: { output_tokens: 98, ... } }</code></pre></div><div class="absolute top-3 right-3 z-10 bg-bg-100 rounded pointer-events-auto transition-opacity duration-200 opacity-100 md:opacity-0 md:group-hover:opacity-100"><button class="inline-flex

Same ID = Same Usage</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">All messages with the same <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">id</code> field report identical usage</strong>. When Claude sends multiple messages in the same turn (e.g., text + tool uses), they share the same message ID and usage data.</p>
<div class="group relative my-5 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><div class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="--shiki-light:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6;--shiki-light-bg:transparent;--shiki-dark-bg:transparent" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">// All these messages have the same ID and usage</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF"> messages</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> [</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">  { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">type:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> 'assistant'</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">id:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> 'msg_123'</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">usage:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">output_tokens:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8"> 100</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> } },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">  { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">type:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> 'assistant'</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">id:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> 'msg_123'</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">usage:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">output_tokens:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8"> 100</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> } },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">  { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">type:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> 'assistant'</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">id:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> 'msg_123'</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">usage:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">output_tokens:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8"> 100</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> } }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">];</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">// Charge only once per unique message ID</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF"> uniqueUsage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> messages</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">[</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">0</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">].</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">usage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">; </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">// Same for all messages with this ID</span></span></code></pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-3 right-3 z-10 bg-bg-100 rounded pointer-events-auto transition-opacity duration-200 opacity-100 md:opacity-0 md:group-hover:opacity-100"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center

<h3 class="text-xl font-medium mb-2 text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6" id="2-charge-once-per-step"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex

Charge Once Per Step</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">You should only charge users once per step</strong>, not for each individual message. When you see multiple assistant messages with the same ID, use the usage from any one of them.</p>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium mb-2 text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6" id="3-result-message-contains-cumulative-usage"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__Ywhj1" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>3. Result Message Contains Cumulative Usage</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">The final <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">result</code> message contains the total cumulative usage from all steps in the conversation:</p>
<div class="group relative my-5 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><div class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="--shiki-light:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6;--shiki-light-bg:transparent;--shiki-dark-bg:transparent" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">// Final result includes total usage</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF"> result</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> query</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">  prompt:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> "Multi-step task"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">  options:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">/* ... */</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">console</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">"Total usage:"</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">result</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">usage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">);</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">class</span><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> CostTracker</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">  private</span><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> processedMessageIds</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> Set</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">&#x3C;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">>();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">  private</span><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> stepUsages</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> Array</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">&#x3C;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0">any</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">> </span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> [];</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">  </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">  async</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> trackConversation</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">prompt</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF"> result</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> query</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">      prompt</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">      options:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">        onMessage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">message</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">=></span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">          this</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">processMessage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">message</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">        }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">      }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">    </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">      result</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">      stepUsages:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe"> this</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">stepUsages</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">      totalCost:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> result</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">usage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">?.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">total_cost_usd</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> ||</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8"> 0</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">    };</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">  </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">  private</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> processMessage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">message</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> any</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">    // Only process assistant messages with usage</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    if</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">message</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> !==</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> 'assistant'</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> ||</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> !</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">message</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">usage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">      return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">    </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">    // Skip if we've already processed this message ID</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    if</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">this</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">processedMessageIds</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">has</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">message</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">)) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">      return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">    </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">    // Mark as processed and record usage</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">    this</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">processedMessageIds</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">add</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">message</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">    this</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">stepUsages</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">push</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">      messageId:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> message</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">id</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">      timestamp:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> Date</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">().</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">toISOString</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(),</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">      usage:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> message</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">usage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">      costUSD:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe"> this</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">calculateCost</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">message</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">usage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">    });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">  </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">  private</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> calculateCost</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">usage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> any</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">)</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">    // Implement your pricing calculation here</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">    // This is a simplified example</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF"> inputCost</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> usage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">input_tokens</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8"> 0.00003</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF"> outputCost</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> usage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">output_tokens</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8"> 0.00015</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">    const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF"> cacheReadCost</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> (</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">usage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">cache_read_input_tokens</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> ||</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8"> 0</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">) </span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">*</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8"> 0.0000075</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">    </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0">    return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> inputCost</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> +</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> outputCost</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> +</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> cacheReadCost</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955">// Usage</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF"> tracker</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA"> CostTracker</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">const</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF">result</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF">stepUsages</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4FC1FF">totalCost</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">=</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#C586C0"> await</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> tracker</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">trackConversation</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">  "Analyze and refactor this code"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">console</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">`Steps processed: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">stepUsages</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">length</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">}</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">console</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">log</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">`Total cost: $</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">${</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">totalCost</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#8250DF;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">toFixed</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#B5CEA8">4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">)</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">}</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178">`</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">);</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div><div data-state="inactive" data-orientation="horizontal" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="radix-_R_mfklubraknmbrkljb_-trigger-1" hidden="" id="radix-_R_mfklubraknmbrkljb_-content-1" tabindex="0" class="codegroup-content"></div></div>
<h2 class="text-2xl font-medium mb-4 text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-8" id="handling-edge-cases"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__Ywhj1" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Handling Edge Cases</div></div></h2>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium mb-2 text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6" id="output-token-discrepancies"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__Ywhj1" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Output Token Discrepancies</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">In rare cases, you might observe different <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">output_tokens</code> values for messages with the same ID. When this occurs:</p>
<ol class="list-none pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item]">
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Use the highest value</strong> - The final message in a group typically contains the accurate total</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Verify against total cost</strong> - The <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">total_cost_usd</code> in the result message is authoritative</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Report inconsistencies</strong> - File issues at the <a class="inline-link" href="https://github.com/anthropics/claude-code/issues">Claude Code GitHub repository</a></li>
</ol>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium mb-2 text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6" id="cache-token-tracking"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">When using prompt caching, track these token types separately:</p>
<div class="group relative my-5 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><div class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="--shiki-light:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6;--shiki-light-bg:transparent;--shiki-dark-bg:transparent" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">interface</span><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> CacheUsage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> {</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">  cache_read_input_tokens</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">  cache_creation</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">    ephemeral_5m_input_tokens</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">    ephemeral_1h_input_tokens</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">;</span></span>

<ol class="list-none pl-8 [counter-reset:item] [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:[counter-reset:item]">
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Use Message IDs for Deduplication</strong>: Always track processed message IDs to avoid double-charging</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Monitor the Result Message</strong>: The final result contains authoritative cumulative usage</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Implement Logging</strong>: Log all usage data for auditing and debugging</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Handle Failures Gracefully</strong>: Track partial usage even if a conversation fails</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Consider Streaming</strong>: For streaming responses, accumulate usage as messages arrive</li>
</ol>

  select-none

  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent

          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__Ywhj1" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Usage Fields Reference</div></div></h2>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Each usage object contains:</p>
<ul class="list-none pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">input_tokens</code>: Base input tokens processed</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">output_tokens</code>: Tokens generated in the response</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">cache_creation_input_tokens</code>: Tokens used to create cache entries</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">cache_read_input_tokens</code>: Tokens read from cache</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">service_tier</code>: The service tier used (e.g., &quot;standard&quot;)</li>
<li class="my-2 relative before:absolute before:left-[-1.5rem] before:w-6 before:text-center before:text-text-500 [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;•&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">total_cost_usd</code>: Total cost in USD (only in result message)</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="text-2xl font-medium mb-4 text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-8" id="example-building-a-billing-dashboard"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Here&#x27;s how to aggregate usage data for a billing dashboard:</p>
<div class="group relative my-5 rounded-lg bg-bg-000 overflow-hidden border-0.5 border-border-300"><div class="relative py-4 pl-4 font-mono text-sm md:text-sm overflow-x-auto code-block-scroll" tabindex="0"><div class="inline-block min-w-full pr-4"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default dark-plus" style="--shiki-light:#1f2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6;--shiki-light-bg:transparent;--shiki-dark-bg:transparent" tabindex="0"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">class</span><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#4EC9B0"> BillingAggregator</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe">  private</span><span style="--shiki-light:#953800;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> userUsage</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#9cdcfe"> new</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE"> Map</span><span style="--shiki-light:#CF222E;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">&#x3C;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#9CDCFE">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#f3f7f6">, {</span></span>

nonce="yYEy6lqEDOSxAmwpRRMHkQ==">self.__next_f.push([1,"from claude_agent_sdk import query, AssistantMessage, ResultMessage\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport asyncio\n\nclass CostTracker:\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.processed_message_ids = set()\n        self.step_usages = []\n\n    async def track_conversation(self, prompt):\n        result = None\n\n        # Process messages as they arrive\n        async for message in query(prompt=prompt):\n            self.process_message(message)\n\n            # Capture the final result message\n            if isinstance(message, ResultMessage):\n                result = message\n\n        return {\n            \"result\": result,\n            \"step_usages\": self.step_usages,\n            \"total_cost\": result.total_cost_usd if result else 0\n        }\n\n    def process_message(self, message):\n        # Only process assistant messages with usage\n        if not isinstance(message, AssistantMessage) or not hasattr(message, 'usage'):\n            return\n\n        # Skip if already processed this message ID\n        message_id = getattr(message, 'id', None)\n        if not message_id or message_id in self.processed_message_ids:\n            return\n\n        # Mark as processed and record usage\n        self.processed_message_ids.add(message_id)\n        self.step_usages.append({\n            \"message_id\": message_id,\n            \"timestamp\": datetime.now().isoformat(),\n            \"usage\": message.usage,\n            \"cost_usd\": self.calculate_cost(message.usage)\n        })\n\n    def calculate_cost(self, usage):\n        # Implement your pricing calculation\n        input_cost = usage.get(\"input_tokens\", 0) * 0.00003\n        output_cost = usage.get(\"output_tokens\", 0) * 0.00015\n        cache_read_cost = usage.get(\"cache_read_input_tokens\", 0) * 0.0000075\n\n        return input_cost + output_cost + cache_read_cost\n\n# Usage\nasync def main():\n    tracker = CostTracker()\n    result = await tracker.track_conversation(\"Analyze and refactor this code\")\n\n    print(f\"Steps processed: {len(result['step_usages'])}\")\n    print(f\"Total cost: ${result['total_cost']:.4f}\")\n\nasyncio.run(main())"])</script><script nonce="yYEy6lqEDOSxAmwpRRMHkQ==">self.__next_f.push([1,"50:T41ed,"])</script><script
